msg:I have stayed in this hotel, I am really speechless, there are two extremes of good and bad.
The location of the hotel is absolutely ok. It's in Yuehe Ancient Town. It's only a few hundred meters away from the ancient town. Moreover, the ancient town is very large and has everything you need to eat, drink and have fun.
The interior facilities of the room are complete, relatively high-end and simple style, the room is also very large, especially the bathroom, which is super large and very comfortable.
The breakfast is a bit simple, not too many varieties, but it's okay, and the dining environment is very good.
To say that there are two things that cannot be tolerated is really too bad.
As soon as I entered the room, I was greeted by a strong musty smell, which made me eager to open the windows and doors to get some air. Half an hour later, the smell was slightly lighter, and I could finally sit down.
Sleeping at night, it is difficult to sleep all night, the temperature is 20 degrees, the air conditioner is useless, and the warm air is 25 degrees, which cannot be adjusted, and it will always be this temperature.
Let‚Äôs talk about the thick and heavy quilt (cotton core) on the bed. It‚Äôs really heavy and hot to cover, and too cold without a cover. I don‚Äôt know what to do! !
After closing the door, the strong musty smell came back again. I was forced to open the curtains and open the windows to ventilate. Even so, the musty smell couldn't be eliminated (I can't let me sleep with the door open all night).
